 This debate is quite old whether the location information of Android users goes to Google
 iske peeche kai tark hai
 First is that Google does not take anything without your permission and second is that you are on Google's platform and how can you think that Google does not know about your location
 baharhaal ham aisa isliye kah rahe hai ki quartz ne ek investigeshan kiya he jisase google lokation sarvice ko lekar kuch baaten saamne aa rahi hai
 According to the investment of American Publication Quartz, Android devices i
e
 smartphones and tabs send the user's location to Google
 ye lokation diarect yujar kaa nahin hota, balki ye cellphone tower kaa lokation hota he
 The shocking disclosure in this is that even if the user has disabled the location, the location of the cellphone tower goes to Google
 Quartz ne kaha he ki jaanch main yah bhi paaya gaya he ki android divaais ko agaraapane factory difolt setting risetubhi kar diya he phir bhi divaais kaa lokation data google ko miltaa rahata he
 Not only this, after this investigation, Quartz has also said that the location sends Google through wifi and cellular data every time it is connected to the nearest tower
 ek doosraa khulaasa ye hua he ki agar divaais main sim nahin bhi ho to lokation bheje jate hai
 These locations are sent based on wifi connectivity
 quartz ke mutabik 2017 kii shuruyaat se hi android smartfones aas paas ke cellular towers kii jaankaree colect kar rahe hai
 This is happening despite the closure of the location service
 cellular data colect karne tak kii baat nahin he, balki ise google ko bheja bhi ja rahaa he
 According to Quartz report, users' location information is given to Google's parent company Alphabet and they get information about the movement of the customers
 quartz ne yah bhi kaha ki is bare main unhone google se sampark kiya he or google ne isaki pushti kii he ki wo aisa karte hai
 However, Google also says that the company does not use the user's location datacollection in this way
 balki is data kaa istemaal karke vigyaapan dene waalon torget customers tak pahunchane main aasaani hoti he
 According to Quartz, for example, through this location tracking, the company can find out when a person using Android is going to which shop

 ) Dengue has broken the 19-year-old record in Delhi
 is saal 10 oktober tak dengue ke 10683 maamalon kii pushti hui he
 Health Department officials said that in the last 19 years, there have never been so many cases of dengue
 adhikariyon ne bataaya ki isse pehle dengue ne 10,000 kaa aankada 1996 main paar kiya tha
 In 1996, 10252 cases of dengue were confirmed in the capital
 dilli se sate uttar pradesh ke shahar gajiabad or haryana ke gudgaanv or faridabad main kul milakar dengue ke 646 maamle saamne aae hai
 According to the latest Delhi Municipal Corporation data, 3077 patients have been confirmed to have dengue in the last one week
 sarkari adhikariyon ke mutabik rashtriya rajdhani main dengue se aadhikarik rup se 30 logon ke marane kii pushti hui he
 But, according to non-government data, 85 patients have died due to dengue this year
 aspataal ke adhikariyon ke mutabik dengue se ravivaar ko ek kishor or ek 41 saal ke aadmi kii maut ho gai

 ke
 Garhpahile said, 'there are more cases of fever in our hospital
 is maamle par kareebi nigaah rakhi jaani chahie

 'tippaniyan He said, 'dengue cases will automatically reduce with increasing cold
 ' a senior doctor at the All India Institute of Medical Sciences (AIIMS) said, 'dengue now seems uncontrollable
 is saal jitne maamle saamne aae hai use dekhte hue yah saaf he ki naagarik prashasan chhidkaav jaise aasaan upayon par hi ab nirbhar nahin rah saktaa

 The land of Jharkhand has been the cradle of tribal culture
 sadiyon se maanav sabhyataa yahaan falti-phoolati rahi he
 The people living in this area are called Adivasis
 yani ki aise nivasee jo lagbhag sabhyataa kii shuruyaat se hi yahaan rahete aae hai
 These tribes became nature sons after harmonizing with nature for hundreds of years
 jangal, nadiyaan pahaad or jharne inaki jindagi main oxigen kii tarah shaamil hai
 There are many castes and sub-castes of tribals in Jharkhand
 jharkhand sarkaar ke mutabik jharkhand main 32 adivasee samooh athwa janajatiyaan rahati hai
 The major groups among these are Munda, Santal, Oraon, Khadia, Gond, Asura, Baiga, Birhor, Godait, Pahadia etc
 munda, santal jaisi janajatiyaan raajnneetik rup se sajag hai
 He has a lot of interference in the politics of Jharkhand
 inaki anuthi paramparaayen or reeti rivaaj hai

 jharkhand main anusuchit janajatiyon kii kul aabaadi kaa aadha se adhik hissaa lohardaga or purvi singhbhum main rahata he

 As soon as someone enters Cooch Behar in West Bengal, the pages of history tell many stories of its deterioration
 kooch bihar bengal ke un loksabhaa siton main se ek he, jo aitihaasik hone ke saath hi prakritik sansadhano or apni khubsuurati ke liye jaani jaati hai

 Later it became part of the Kamata Empire
 kamta samrajya par sabase pehle khen rajwans kaa raaj rahaa jinaki rajdhani kamtapur hua karti thi

 The partition of the Kamata Empire into Cooch Behar and Koch Hajo was permanent

 Rashmirathi is an epic work of Hindi literature, an epic
 yah saal 1952 main rashtrakavi ke rup main pratishthit ho chuke kavi ramdhaari singh 'dinakar' dwaara likhi gai thi
 It centers around the life of Karna, a great character in the epic Vyasa Mahabharata
 karn avivaahit kunti, jo baad main pandu kii patni baniin, kaa putr tha
 Kunti left her eldest son at birth as he was a child of premarital, whom Kunti could never adopt due to social fear
 karn kaa paalan-poshan ek nimna parivaar main hua, phir bhi vah apane kaushal, swabhaav va shaury se us samay ke sarvshereshth yoddhaon main se ek ban gaya
 The battle of Karna on behalf of the Kauravdal during the Mahabharata war was a major concern for the Pandavas, as he was reputed to be invincible in battle
 is tarah se dinakar us samooche kaal kaa varnan behad rochak dhang se kiya he
 The way he presents the story of Karna with all shades of human emotions trapped in moral dilemmas is amazing in itself

 *** September 1 means that breaking the rules while driving from today can be very heavy on your pocket as the Motor Vehicle Act 2019 has come into force from today
 is act main jurmaane main baari izaafaa kiya gaya he
 According to the new rule, a fine of Rs 25,000 and driving registration of a minor will be canceled
 bina helmet ke dupahiyaa vaahan chalaane par 500 se 1500 rupee kaa jurmaana
 Earlier it was 100 to 300 rupees
 dupahiyaa vaahan par teen sawari baitaane par jo jurmaana pehle 100 rupee tha ab wo 500 rupee ho gaya he
 In the absence of pollution certificate, earlier Rs 100 had to be paid, now Rs 500 will have to be paid
 bina driving license ke gaadi chalaate paae jane par ab 500 kii jagah 5000 ru dene honge
 For dangerous driving, now you have to pay 5 thousand rupees instead of one thousand
 driving ke dauraan phone par baat karne par 1 hazaar kii jagah 5 hazaar rupee tak bharne padenge
 For driving in the wrong direction, now you have to pay Rs 5000 instead of 1100
 
 The penalty earlier on jumping red light was only 100 rupees, now it has become 10 thousand
 seat belt lagaae bina gaadi chalaane par ab 1 hazaar rupye kaa jurmaana bharna padegaa
 The fine for driving drunk is now increased to 10 thousand
 immergency gadiyon jaise ambulance or damakal kii gadiyon ko said na dene par 10 hazaar ru kaa jurmaana dena hoga
